# Faction leader convenes a meeting
character_event = {
	id = 1000182465
	picture = "GFX_evt_emissary"

	desc = "EVTDESC1900500"

	trigger = {
		had_global_flag = {
			flag = startup
			days = 730
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_meeting_called }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed }
			had_character_flag = {
				flag = faction_meeting_postponed
				days = 730
			}
			AND = {
				had_character_flag = {
					flag = faction_meeting_postponed
					days = 365
				}
				NOT = {
					liege = {
						any_war = {
							defender = {
								character = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry 
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_court_angry 
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry 
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_meeting }
			had_character_flag = {
				flag = faction_meeting
				days = 1095
			}
			AND = {
				had_character_flag = {
					flag = faction_meeting
					days = 730
				}
				NOT = {
					liege = {
						any_war = {
							defender = {
								character = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry 
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_court_angry 
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry 
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry 
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		any_faction_backer = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_king
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
					in_faction = faction_republican_king
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
					in_faction = faction_republican_duke
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
					in_faction = faction_religious_king
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
					in_faction = faction_religious_duke
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_court_emperor
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
					in_faction = faction_court_king
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
					in_faction = faction_court_duke
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 48
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.05
			OR = {
				has_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
				had_character_flag = {
					flag = faction_meeting
					days = 2555
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			NOT = {
				liege = {
					any_war = {
						defender = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry 
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_court_king
						leads_faction = faction_court_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_court_angry 
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_religious_king
						leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry 
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_republican_king
						leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry 
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900500"
		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }
		set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 0 }
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP51 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP52 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP53 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP54 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1000182467 }
			}
			character_event = { id = 1000182468 days = 7 } # regular meeting
			character_event = { id = 1000182469 days = 7 } # angry meeting
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB1900500"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 0.5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 1.5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 2.5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 3.5 }
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP50 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 0.5 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 1.5 } }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				character_event = { id = 1000182466 tooltip = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 1.5 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 2.5 } }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				character_event = { id = 1000182466 tooltip = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 2.5 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 3.5 } }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 75
				character_event = { id = 1000182466 tooltip = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 3.5 }
			}
			character_event = { id = 1000182466 tooltip = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
		}
		change_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 1 }
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 1000182466
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"

	desc = "EVTDESC1900501"

	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1000182483 } #notify
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = former_faction_leader
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900501"
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = count
			}
			prestige = -100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = duke
			}
			prestige = -200
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = king
			}
			prestige = -400
		}
	}
}

	desc = "EVTDESC1900502"

		name = "EVTOPTA1900502"
	}
}

# Regular meeting - setting the agenda
character_event = {
	id = 1000182468
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"

	desc = "EVTDESC1900503"

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		has_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}
					liege = {
						OR = {
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_unhappy
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_court_king
						leads_faction = faction_court_duke
					}
					liege = {
						OR = {
							has_character_flag = faction_court_unhappy
							has_character_flag = faction_court_angry
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_religious_king
						leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}
					liege = {
						OR = {
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_unhappy
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_republican_king
						leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}
					liege = {
						OR = {
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_unhappy
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
		any_faction_backer = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_king
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
					in_faction = faction_republican_king
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
					in_faction = faction_republican_duke
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
					in_faction = faction_religious_king
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
					in_faction = faction_religious_duke
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_court_emperor
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
					in_faction = faction_court_king
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
					in_faction = faction_court_duke
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge_defeated
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900503"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {

				trait = content
			}

				factor = 0.75
				trait = charitable
			}
		}
		character_event = { id = 1000182487 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900600 } #strengthen own position
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB1900503"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = humble

			}

				opinion = { who = liege value = 100 }

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				opinion = { who = liege value = 25 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5

			}
			modifier = {

			}
		}
		character_event = { id = 1000182488 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900601 } #strengthen liege
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC1900503"

# Angry meeting - setting the agenda
character_event = {
	id = 1000182469
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		has_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		OR = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor

					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke

				OR = {

					leads_faction = faction_court_duke
				}
				liege = {
					OR = {
						has_character_flag = faction_court_unhappy
						has_character_flag = faction_court_angry
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
				}
				liege = {
					OR = {
						has_character_flag = faction_religious_unhappy

					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTF1900504"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP59 }
		trigger = {
			liege = {
				any_war = {
					defender = {
						character = PREVPREV
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_court_king
						leads_faction = faction_court_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_court_angry
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_religious_king
						leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_republican_king
						leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
	}
}

# Faction leader is ousted after losing a regular vote
character_event = {
	id = 1000182470
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"

	desc = "EVTDESC1900505"

	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1000182484 } #notify
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = former_faction_leader
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900505"
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = count
			}
			prestige = -100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = duke
			}
			prestige = -200
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = king
			}
			prestige = -400
		}
	}
}

# Faction leader is ousted after wasting a meeting
character_event = {
	id = 1000182481
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"

	desc = "EVTDESC1900516"

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = former_faction_leader
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1000182485 } #notify
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900516"
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = count
			}
			prestige = -100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = duke
			}
			prestige = -200
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = king
			}
			prestige = -400
		}
	}
}

# Great speech
character_event = {
	id = 1000182491
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"

	desc = "EVTDESC1900700"

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900700"
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = count
			}
			prestige = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = duke
			}
			prestige = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = king
			}
			prestige = 200
		}
		any_faction_backer = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
						in_faction = faction_republican_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
						in_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
						in_faction = faction_religious_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
						in_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_court_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
						in_faction = faction_court_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
						in_faction = faction_court_duke
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = great_speech
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = good_speech
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = okay_speech
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = bad_speech
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = terrible_speech
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = great_speech
				years = 10
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182492 } } #notify
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 1000182499
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"

	desc = "EVTDESC1900708"

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900708"

			limit = {
				tier = count
			}
			prestige = -50
		}

			limit = {
				tier = duke
			}
			prestige = -100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = king
			}
			prestige = -200
		}
		set_character_flag = former_faction_leader
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
		any_faction_backer = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
						in_faction = faction_republican_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
						in_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
						in_faction = faction_religious_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
						in_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_court_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
						in_faction = faction_court_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
						in_faction = faction_court_duke
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = great_speech
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = good_speech
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = okay_speech
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = bad_speech
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = terrible_speech
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = terrible_speech
				years = 10
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182500 } } #notify
		}
	}
}

# Faction leader wants money - result of the vote
character_event = {
	id = 1000182501
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"

	desc = "EVTDESC1900710"

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900710"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -0.5 }
		}
		set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		any_faction_backer = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
						in_faction = faction_republican_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
						in_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
						in_faction = faction_religious_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
						in_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_court_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
						in_faction = faction_court_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
						in_faction = faction_court_duke
					}
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { tier = king } ROOT = { wealth = 30 } }
			if = { limit = { tier = duke } ROOT = { wealth = 20 } }
			if = { limit = { tier = count } ROOT = { wealth = 10 } }
		}
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }
		}
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king

						AND = {

							in_faction = faction_court_emperor

							in_faction = faction_court_king

							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }

						}

							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke

							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}

							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1000182505 } #notify
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = FEUDALFACTIONMOODPLUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_feudal" value = 3 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 1000183004 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182506 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = COURTFACTIONMOODPLUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_court" value = 3 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 1000183004 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182506 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor

			}
			liege = {

					text = REPUBLICANFACTIONMOODPLUS

					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182506 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = RELIGIOUSFACTIONMOODPLUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_religious" value = 3 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 1000183004 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182506 } } #notify
				}

		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting

							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1000182508 } #notify
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = FEUDALFACTIONMOODPLUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_feudal" value = 1 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 1000183004 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182509 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = COURTFACTIONMOODPLUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_court" value = 1 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 1000183004 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182509 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = REPUBLICANFACTIONMOODPLUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_republican" value = 1 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 1000183004 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182509 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = RELIGIOUSFACTIONMOODPLUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_religious" value = 1 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 1000183004 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182509 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
	}
}

# Decreased faction opinion of liege
character_event = {
	id = 1000182510
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"

	desc = "EVTDESC1900719"

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900719"
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1000182511 } #notify
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_court_angry
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 75
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182470 days = 3 } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_unhappy
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_court_unhappy
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_unhappy
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_unhappy
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182470 days = 3 } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_feudal_unhappy
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_court_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_court_unhappy
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_religious_unhappy
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_republican_unhappy

					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 20
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182470 days = 3 } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = FEUDALFACTIONMOODMINUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_feudal" value = -3 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 1000183004 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182512 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = COURTFACTIONMOODMINUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_court" value = -3 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 1000183004 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182512 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {

				OR = {

					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke

# Faction leader wants money for liege - result of the vote
character_event = {
	id = 1000182513
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"

	desc = "EVTDESC1900722"

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900722"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -0.5 }
		}
		set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		if = { limit = { tier = king } wealth = -30 }
		if = { limit = { tier = duke } wealth = -20 }
		if = { limit = { tier = count } wealth = -10 }
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }
		}
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1000182514 } #notify
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = 1000182940 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPGIFT } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
				}
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = 1000182958 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPGIFT } }
		}
		if = {

# Yes vote - notify
character_event = {
	id = 1000182514
	is_triggered_only = yes

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"

	desc = "EVTDESC1900723"

	option = {
		name = "OK"
		if = { limit = { tier = king } wealth = -30 }
		if = { limit = { tier = duke } wealth = -20 }
		if = { limit = { tier = count } wealth = -10 }
		FROM = {
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = FROM
						modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }
			}
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = FROM
						modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47 }
			}
		}
	}
}

							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 20
				custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182470 days = 3 } }
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
	}
}

# Yes vote - notify
character_event = {
	id = 1000182517
	is_triggered_only = yes

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"

	desc = "EVTDESC1900726"

	trigger = {
		ai = no
	}

	option = {
		name = "OK"
		FROM = {
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = FROM
						modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }
			}
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = FROM
						modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47 }
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = 1000182519
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"

	desc = "EVTDESC1900728"

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900728"
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1000182520 } #notify
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = FEUDALFACTIONMOODMINUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_feudal" value = -3 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 1000183004 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182521 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = COURTFACTIONMOODMINUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_court" value = -3 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 1000183004 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182521 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = REPUBLICANFACTIONMOODMINUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_republican" value = -3 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 1000183004 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182521 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = RELIGIOUSFACTIONMOODMINUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_religious" value = -3 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 1000183004 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182521 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
	}

				chance = 50
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182470 days = 3 } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_feudal_unhappy
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_court_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_court_unhappy
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_religious_unhappy
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_republican_unhappy
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 20
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182470 days = 3 } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = FEUDALFACTIONMOODPLUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_feudal" value = 3 }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = 1000183004 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182527 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = COURTFACTIONMOODPLUS
					change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_court" value = 3 }

					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = 1000182527 } } #notify
				}
			}

					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor

# Faction leader wants to declare war - results of the vote
character_event = {
	id = 1000182528
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"

	desc = "EVTDESC1900737"

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900737"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -0.5 }
		}
		set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }
		}
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1000182529 } #notify
			}
		}
		liege = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {
					set_character_flag = faction_feudal_war
					ROOT = {
						add_trait = rebel hidden_tooltip = { opinion = { who = LIEGE modifier = revolting_against years = 100 } }
						any_faction_backer = {
							faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							add_trait = rebel hidden_tooltip = { opinion = { who = LIEGE modifier = revolting_against years = 100 } }
						}
					}
				}
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = cb_faction_overthrow_ruler
					faction = faction_feudal_emperor
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {
					set_character_flag = faction_feudal_war
					ROOT = {
						add_trait = rebel hidden_tooltip = { opinion = { who = LIEGE modifier = revolting_against years = 100 } }
						any_faction_backer = {
							faction = faction_feudal_king
							add_trait = rebel hidden_tooltip = { opinion = { who = LIEGE modifier = revolting_against years = 100 } }
						}
					}
				}
				reverse_war = {

				}
			}

							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}

							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}

							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}

							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1000182530 } #notify

# Faction leader wants to demand lower CA - results of the vote
character_event = {
	id = 1000182531
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"

	desc = "EVTDESC1900740"

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900740"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -0.5 }
		}
		set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = 1000182937 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
				}
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = 1000182956 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
				}
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = 1000182950 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }
		}
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }
		}
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}

	hide_from = yes

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"

	desc = "EVTDESC1900746"

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA1900746"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -0.5 }
		}
		set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = 1000182943 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
				}
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = 1000182961 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }

					leads_faction = faction_court_duke

			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = 1000182562 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }
		}
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46 }
		}
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king

							in_faction = faction_republican_king

							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor

						AND = {

							in_faction = faction_religious_king

							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}

							in_faction = faction_court_emperor

							in_faction = faction_court_duke

					}

# Oust faction leader
character_event = {
	id = 1000182546

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"

	desc = "EVTDESC1900800"

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		has_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge_defeated }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 6
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { prestige = 0 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { diplomacy = 10 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			diplomacy = 20
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { prestige = 500 }
			any_faction_backer = {
				prestige = 500
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { prestige = 1000 }
			any_faction_backer = {
				prestige = 1000
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { prestige = 2000 }
			any_faction_backer = {
				prestige = 2000
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			OR = {
				leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
				leads_faction = faction_religious_king
				leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			}
			NOT = { piety = 0 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_faction_backer = {
				higher_tier_than = ROOT
				OR = {
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
						in_faction = faction_republican_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
						in_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
						in_faction = faction_religious_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
						in_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_court_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
						in_faction = faction_court_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
						in_faction = faction_court_duke
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {

		set_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge

						}

						AND = {

					}

	}

						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = 1000182550 } #notify
			}
		}
	}
}
